select @t = type, @id = id from sysobjects where name = @name declare @rst varchar(max); set @rst = &&&; if(@t = &&&) BEGIN    select @rst = &&& + CHAR(#)+ CHAR(#) END ELSE IF (@t = &&&) BEGIN    select @rst = &&& + CHAR(#)+ CHAR(#) END ELSE IF (@t = &&&) BEGIN    select @rst = &&& + CHAR(#)+ CHAR(#) END ELSE IF (@t = &&&) BEGIN    select @rst = &&& + CHAR(#)+ CHAR(#) END ELSE IF (@t = &&&) BEGIN    select @rst = &&& + CHAR(#)+ CHAR(#) END  if(@t = &&& or @t = &&& or @t = &&& or @t = &&& or @t = &&&)BEGIN    select @rst = @rst + cast(&&& as char(#))+cast(&&& as char(#))+cast(&&& as char(#))+ CHAR(#)+CHAR(#);    select 			@rst = @rst+cast(name as char(#)), 			@rst = @rst+cast(type_name(user_type_id) as char(#)), 			@rst = @rst+cast(max_length as varchar(#)) + CHAR(#) 	from sys.all_parameters where object_id = @id 	order by parameter_id END ELSE BEGIN 	select @rst = @rst + sc.text  	from syscomments sc, sysobjects so 	where so.name = @name and sc.id = so.id END select @rst;

SELECT     Genre.Name, MediaType.Name  FROM chinook.TRACK     INNER JOIN chinook.Genre.Name  on chinook.Track.GenreId=chinook.Genre.GenreId     Inner JOIN chinook.MediaType.Name on chinook.Track.MediaTypeId=chinook.MediaType.MediaTypeId
SELECT     Genre.Name, MediaType.Name  FROM chinook.TRACK     chinook.Genre.Name INNER JOIN on chinook.Track.GenreId=chinook.Genre.GenreId     chinook.MediaType.Name Inner JOIN on chinook.Track.MediaTypeId=chinook.MediaType.MediaTypeId
SELECT     chinook.Genre.Name as GenreM, chinook.MediaType.Name as MediaTypeN FROM chinook.TRACK     chinook.Genre.Name INNER JOIN on chinook.Track.GenreId=chinook.Genre.GenreId     chinook.MediaType.Name Inner JOIN on chinook.Track.MediaTypeId=chinook.MediaType.MediaTypeId
SELECT     Genre.Name as GenreM, MediaType.Name as MediaTypeN FROM      chinook.Genre.Name INNER JOIN on chinook.Track.GenreId=chinook.Genre.GenreId     chinook.MediaType.Name Inner JOIN on chinook.Track.MediaTypeId=chinook.MediaType.MediaTypeId
SELECT     Genre.Name as Genre, MediaType.Name as MediaTypeN FROM      chinook.Genre.Name INNER JOIN on chinook.Track.GenreId=chinook.Genre.GenreId     chinook.MediaType.Name Inner JOIN on chinook.Track.MediaTypeId=chinook.MediaType.MediaTypeId
SELECT     Genre.Name as Genre, MediaType.Name as MediaType FROM      chinook.Genre.Name INNER JOIN on chinook.Track.GenreId=chinook.Genre.GenreId     chinook.MediaType.Name Inner JOIN on chinook.Track.MediaTypeId=chinook.MediaType.MediaTypeId
SELECT     chinook.Genre.Name as Genre, chinook.MediaType.Name as MediaType FROM      chinook.Genre.Name INNER JOIN on chinook.Track.GenreId=chinook.Genre.GenreId     chinook.MediaType.Name Inner JOIN on chinook.Track.MediaTypeId=chinook.MediaType.MediaTypeId
SELECT      chinook.Genre.Name, chinook.MediaType.Name FROM      chinook.Genre   CROSS JOIN      chinook.MediaType;
SELECT      a.f, b.g FROM      chinook.Genre.Name AS a    CROSS JOIN      chinook.MediaType.Name AS b;
SELECT      a.f, b.g FROM      chinook.Genre AS a    CROSS JOIN      chinook.MediaType AS b;
SELECT      a.Name, b.Name FROM      chinook.Genre AS a    CROSS JOIN      chinook.MediaType AS b;
SELECT      a, b FROM      chinook.Genre.Name AS a    CROSS JOIN      chinook.MediaType.Name AS b;
SELECT      a.name,  b.name  FROM      chinook.Genre AS a    CROSS JOIN      chinook.MediaType AS b;
SELECT      chinook.Genre.Name, chinook.MediaType.Name  FROM      chinook.Genre AS a    CROSS JOIN      chinook.MediaType AS b;
select SUBSTRING(Name, #, #) AS FirstLetter from chinook.Artist group by FirstLetter;

SELECT TOP # fld.run, fld.avg_sky_muJy, fld.runarea AS area, ISNULL(fp.nfirstmatch,#)  FROM (   SELECT run, sum(primaryArea) AS runarea,  #e6*avg(power(cast(#. as float),#*sky_r)) as avg_sky_muJy  FROM Field  GROUP BY run  ) AS fld  LEFT OUTER JOIN (   SELECT p.run, count(*) AS nfirstmatch  FROM FIRST AS fm  INNER JOIN photoprimary as p  ON p.objid=fm.objid  GROUP BY p.run  ) AS fp  ON fld.run=fp.run  ORDER BY fld.run
